GT Equivalence Verification (BPG22)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - exp(-c2*P))*P + c3*P*exp(-c4*t)
Candidate formulas: 123

GT (fixed):
\[
f(t,P)=0.1178160925\,(1-e^{-0.02722849124\,P})\,P \;+\;0.1178160925\,P\,e^{-0.02722849124\,t}
\]
Rewrite structure:
\[
f(t,P)=0.1178160925\,P \;-\;0.1178160925\,P\,e^{-kP}\;+\;0.1178160925\,P\,e^{-kt},\quad k=0.02722849124
\]
So GT is a sum of three terms: (i) linear in \(P\), (ii) \(P\exp(\text{linear in }P)\) with **negative** exponent and **no Abs(P)**, and (iii) \(P\exp(\text{linear in }t)\) with **negative** exponent.

Necessary matching requirements for any candidate:
1) Must contain a \(P\exp(\alpha P)\) term (not \(\exp(\alpha|P|)\), not \(\exp(\alpha t)\)) to represent \(-0.1178\,P e^{-kP}\).
2) Must contain a \(P\exp(\beta t)\) term to represent \(+0.1178\,P e^{-kt}\).
3) Must not introduce extra nonzero terms (constants, sin, log, Max, rational terms, etc.), unless their coefficients can be set to 0.
4) Any use of \(\mathrm{Abs}(P)\) is fatal because GT is not an even function of \(P\) in the exponential term: \(P e^{-kP}\neq P e^{-k|P|}\) for negative \(P\).

Now check candidates.

1. \(P c0 + P c1 e^{Pc2} + P c3\sin(\cdot) + P c6 e^{c7 t} + P c8\).  
   Can zero out sine: \(c3=0\). Combine linear terms: \(Pc0+Pc8\). Has \(P e^{Pc2}\) and \(P e^{c7 t}\). This matches GT’s needed functional forms. Choose:
   - \(c2=-k\)
   - \(c1=-0.1178160925\)
   - \(c7=-k\)
   - \(c6=+0.1178160925\)
   - \(c0+c8=+0.1178160925\)
   Then candidate equals GT for all \(t,P\). **Matches.**

2. Has \(P e^{c2 t}\) and \(P e^{c8|P|}\) and sine. Abs(P) term cannot become \(P e^{-kP}\) for all \(P\). Even if \(c7=0\) to remove it, then you lose the required \(P e^{-kP}\) term. **No match.**

3. Same issue: \(P e^{c4|P|}\) instead of \(P e^{cP}\). **No match.**

4. \(P c0 e^{Pc1} + P c2 + P c3\sin(\cdot) + P c6 e^{c7 t} + c8\).  
   Set \(c3=0\), \(c8=0\). Then has \(P e^{Pc1}\), linear \(P\), and \(P e^{c7 t}\). Choose:
   - \(c1=-k\)
   - \(c0=-0.1178160925\)
   - \(c7=-k\)
   - \(c6=+0.1178160925\)
   - \(c2=+0.1178160925\)
   **Matches.**

5. Has \(P e^{Pc2}\) and \(P e^{c4 t}\) plus log term and constant. Set log coefficient \(c6=0\) and constant \(c5=0\). Then reduces to \(Pc0 + P c1 e^{Pc2} + P c3 e^{c4 t}\). + c9)"]

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: c0*(c1 - exp(-c2*P))*P + c3*P*exp(-c4*t)**

With numerical values: `0.11781609251252895*(1 - exp(-0.027228491244958825*P))*P + 0.11781609251252895*P*exp(-0.027228491244958825*t)`

Expanding: `0.11781609251252895*P - 0.11781609251252895*P*exp(-0.027228491244958825*P) + 0.11781609251252895*P*exp(-0.027228491244958825*t)`

So GT = **A*P + B*P*exp(-α*P) + C*P*exp(-β*t)** where A > 0, B < 0, α > 0, β > 0.

The key structural components are:
1. A linear term in P: `const * P`
2. `P * exp(negative_const * P)` term
3. `P * exp(negative_const * t)` term

Let me check each candidate systematically. I'll focus on whether each candidate's functional form can match these three basis functions exactly.

**Key observations:**
- `exp(c*P)` with c < 0 matches `exp(-α*P)` ✓
- `exp(c*Abs(P))` with P ≥ 0 equals `exp(c*P)` ✓ (domain constraint)
- Extra additive constants (not multiplied by P) cannot be absorbed unless set to 0
- Extra terms like `sin(...)`, `log(...)`, `t`, `t^c`, `Max(...)`, `P^c` etc. that aren't in GT must be eliminable (set to 0)

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + P*c3*sin(c4 + c5*t) + P*c6*exp(c7*t) + P*c8`
- Has P*sin(c4+c5*t) - set c3=0 to eliminate. Remaining: P*(c0+c8) + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + P*c6*exp(c7*t). Matches GT structure. ✓
Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + P*c7*exp(c8*Abs(P))`
- Set c4=0. Remaining: P*(c0+c3) + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c7*exp(c8*P). Matches. ✓
Candidate 2 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3*exp(c4*Abs(P)) + P*c5*sin(c6*t + c7)`
- Set c5=0. Remaining: P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3*exp(c4*P). Matches. ✓

- Need to eliminate the log term and c5. Set c5=0, c6=0. Remaining: P*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + P*c3*exp(c4*t). Matches. ✓
